#  [](/thread/5672-ej4h-method)EJ_4H method 

  * 

  * [#1](/thread/5672-ej4h-method "Post Permalink")

  * First Post: Edited Jun 21, 2006 6:22pm  Apr 13, 2006 8:26am | Edited Jun 21, 2006 6:22pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

I will stop posting here from 23 June 2006 but never stop helping and answering questions. You have my email address at the bottom of all the EJ_4H Method parts .

**Ibo**

\- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -

**This is a forex trading system on H4 chart with attached indicators and templates.**

  
  
**Instructions:**  
  
1- You should use MT4.  
  
2- You should Update Monthly, Weekly, Daily, H4, H1 charts when using.  
  
3- You should copy the indicators in .../Meta Trader/experts/indicators folder.  
  
4- You should copy the indicators in .../Meta Trader/templates folder.  
  
5- As this is an easy-to-use method you just use templates to do every thing with this method.(e.g. ususally setup ej_4h for monitoring and when you are predicting market by pivots you setup ej_4h_wp or/and ej_4h_mp and after your calculation back to ej_4h to see the chart with less difficulty.  
  
6- Templates with the extention of "wb" are ones with White Background to facilitate preparing a picture for printing or other use.  
  
**_Abbreviations:_**  
  
ej_4h ------------------------ Basic template (setup)  
ej_4h_wp -------------------- Basic setup+weekly pivots  
ej_4h_mp -------------------- Basic setup+monthly pivots  
ej_4h_dual stoch ------------- Basic setup+dual stochastic oscillator  
ej_4h dual stoch_Lindsay ----- Basic setup+overlaid dual stochastic oscillator  
  
**_Important Notes:_**  
  
  
**1- All Updates of indicators, templates and documents will be done in this post (the first #1), just a notification will be sent as a new reply (post).**  
  
  
**2-The texts/posts in blue color are the ones that members discuss daily/current price action, forecasts and commentaries; so for shortening the duration of following the thread if you are new to thread you can neglect them for awhile. ( We do this not to distract or diversify the efforts of members by starting a new thread, so please be aware that no new thread related to this method should be started)**  

\- - - - - - - - - - - - - -

**Private Mentoring is available, for more info email to **[[b]ejeddi@gmail.com[/b]](mailto:ejeddi@gmail.com)  

\- - - - - - - - - - - - - -

**You can find the part IV at the address below:**  
[http://www.forexfactory.com/forexfor...1513#post61513](http://www.forexfactory.com/forexforum/showthread.php?p=61513#post61513)

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar3139_4.gif) MikeG](mikeg)

  * | Joined Aug 2005  | Status: Empowered to Profit by James16.com | [59 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=3139)

Thank you for sharing your system. I have no doubt it works because of it's similarity to the Vegas 4 hour model, and Dial's Knife system, both of which are very successful. The reason I appreciate your sharing is that it caused me to view the two abovementioned systems in a slightly different light.  
  
Your repeated mention of distance between the SMA's reminded me of the way Dial describes how every marble in a bag of a marbles is a potential winner and a potential loser and the probability of which it will be is a function of both selected trade direction and distance between the SMA's.  
  
I do have one question though. Are your two SMA's based on the close? I ask because in the Vegas and Knife systems the 55 is based on the median, while the 8 is based on the close.  
  
Thanks!  
  
  
Michele UU 

I am an extremely satisfied customer of the James16 Group!!!

Thanks for the interest, I have to tell you that this is a basic and I did not elaborate it so much because I wanted let poeple develop and implement it as they like, this let them be congenial with the method.  
  
I will let you know if you have any specific question or need personal help to implement or filter, little by little I will add some additional indicators or templates or discuss examples that explain master entries and money managements.  
  
Just keep in mind that:1-We neglect most of the time the bar that bears arrow (signal indicator) 2-when the bar have a very high range (regarding currency pair) be aware because there would be an abnormal reason that it happned, normally there will be a retrace, in such cases enter in/after retracement 3-About the performance in fact we never trust so much to back tests, because the markets always change the behavior and for such shorter time periods any fund can be lost in a medium run, for example try thid method for recent GOLD chart, you see, it is very great, but the behavior of GOLD is complicated and different from forex 4-SMAs are on close, any other setting may differ slightly but the tenets are the same  
  
More in near future,  
Thanks all  
Ibo

I will complete this method in future, I have the plan to add trading tricks with this method almost one time per 2 weeks.  
Dr Rock! defining a trend in a specific time scale is one the most difficult works in trending markets, if somebody can do this easily he can be a millionaire just in some years. On the other hand reversal trading is better and more profitable, there are differences between trend following method and reversal method. This method is reversal type; in this method you are surier about the entry rather than trend following and the risk-reward ratio is higher too. So you don't need to define the trend you just pinpoint where trend reverse and then enter. Look at open/close prices and the 8SMA and then you can find out how the colors apear.  
  
Have a good day  
Ibo

  * [ zzz](zzz)

  * | Joined Apr 2006  | Status: Trader | [159 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=8259)

_Why are there 2 different templates in your file? To me, they look the same. Why two?_  
  
_The difference is that one is with PP, you in some cases will need to use pivot points to see where is the resistances, supports and totally the important levels to put your stops and targets_ __  
  
_2.__What do you think if I use fibo lines from vegas 4-hour as exit points? Why you almost used the first part of vegas system but removed his idea of taking profits at fibo lines? I think one of the huge benefits of vegas system is that it is much easier to exit without second guessing. What is your concept of exit?_  
  
_Many systems are similar in basics but different in details, Vegas 4hr system is good, but its taking direction from weekly chart is not really so profitable, you will lose many of good opportunities.___  
  
_I mentioned the yellow line is the first target that you may use, targeting/risk management is the most important role in trading, I found this after many defeats in trading even with good methods, as I told this is a starting and I will expand it and will tell you many things with real examples, some of them are about money management during holding positions and where you should put stops/TPs. Please be patient but for the time being use whatever you like (I have told this too)___  
  
_3.__When you are saying (page 1): until candles are above or below the white line… you mean the whole candle or just the close?_  
  
_I will publish about this too in detail, but keep in mind when they are regularly are above white line, this is a good and less violate trend (like recent eurgbp moves) but when they are get far form white line they will retrace and touch that frequently until in one case cross it and reverse, in some cases when we don't have a decent trend you see that they cross the white line in some cases and are not decent, many green candles are so but shortly among prices, CLOSE PRICE is the most important, you should include that in most of your considerations or analysis_ __  
  
_4.__My always bottleneck is a proper entry and stop/loss. You are saying in PDF file: always trail the price with a good range. Could you please help me to understand what the good range is? I am really having problems with it. If you could give me some numbers for different currencies, I would be completely happy. I understand this is beyond the scope of just the questions about your method. For now, I am thinking 100 pips for GBP/USD, for example, is a good range. Or this is too much? I am getting tired of being stopped out but I do not want to overshoot either._  
  
___It is not about pips or pairs, it is about corrections and the important major/minor levels that the price during its way come across or build, don't worry I will explain it in advance in future, just easily try to put your_ ___stop beyond the highest high/lowest low and trail it not by trailing stop 100 like this: When a correction done update your stop loss, go H1 and you will see it easily, use PP if they are close to these levels_  
  
___5.__What currencies you think are better to use with EJ?_  
  
_It does not matter, back to the history and see which you are relax with this method, when I were a newbie I used to minor trading because they are less violate, majors are more complicated but more profitable too, use pairs that have decent trends, you can think about markets except forex too, just check them out_ __

Ok, eurusdtrader, here is my next set of questions:  
  
  
  
1. I applied both templates to several currencies and only EUR/USD shows PPs, support and resistance lines. Is it me again, or I have to turn it somehow on?  
  
2. I can see the time, I guess, to the close of the candle. You did not explain what to do with the time. I think you are planning to do it later, right? The time is not moving, it is stuck on 110 min 38 sec, and again, it is only on EUR/USD.  
  
3. You said that the primary target is the cross with the yellow line (55 SMA). What is a secondary target if I don’t have PP, support and resistance on other charts? The opposite signal or the close of the candle on the opposite side of the white line? Your sell signal is a signal to enter a sell trade or exit the previous buy as well?  
  
4. Please, correct me if I am wrong here: you are saying we will often miss the first candle, which is often a big one. This means we will be entering on the retracement. And this is best done by switching to the lower time frame (1H) and entering on the breakout. I would really appreciate if you could publish a chart to show me how you do it with your comments. Would you use just fibo or something trickier to define that entry point? If you were to use an Entry Stop where would you place it?  
  
  
  
To be continued and thank you again.

  * [#15](/thread/post/51821#post51821 "Post Permalink")

  * Apr 17, 2006 4:18pm  Apr 17, 2006 4:18pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

I will tell how to use traditional methods and chart patterns to minimize the risk and enter sooner than getting arrow signals  
  
About the alarm: it is already done, I will post the template in 24 hrs.  
  
  
1.I applied both templates to several currencies and only EUR/USD shows PPs, support and resistance lines. Is it me again, or I have to turn it somehow on?  
Please update your weekly charts too, as you see I give example of many diverse pairs to show that this is not for a specific currency pair  
  
2.I can see the time, I guess, to the close of the candle. You did not explain what to do with the time. I think you are planning to do it later, right? The time is not moving, it is stuck on 110 min 38 sec, and again, it is only on EUR/USD.  
  
  
  
It will be changed when changing the quotes (refresh), you are right about what it shows, just I intensively recommend WAIT FOR CLOSONG THE CANDLE, so in many cases that price move in your direction you will be rash to enter especially when you see the arrow signal and high momentum (fast moving price), but this is killer because before closing the current candle entering a position may harm your deposit as is so volatile and can change its direction just in some minutes. Please regard that we have many specific prices in a candle like opening, high, low, close and so on, but the close price is the most important and professionals always bring it into all their consideration   
  
3.You said that the primary target is the cross with the yellow line (55 SMA). What is a secondary target if I don’t have PP, support and resistance on other charts? The opposite signal or the close of the candle on the opposite side of the white line? Your sell signal is a signal to enter a sell trade or exit the previous buy as well?  
  
I will publish more in detail about the targets, stops and risk management with this method in future, I see that all you are a bit rash to discover everything but market trading needs a GREAT PATIENCE; I appreciate your interests to explore the whole method.  
  
In reversal trading a buy position closes with a sell signal and vice versa, but all these signals are not eligible to enter, so shortly in most of the time a contrary signal is an exit signal but about entering short (sell) you should have enough reasons.  
  
  
  
(e.g. you are long and see a sell signal the it is better to exit but if you have knowledgeable about trading and money management you can hold the position but minimize the risk)   
  
  
  
4.Please, correct me if I am wrong here: you are saying we will often miss the first candle, which is often a big one. This means we will be entering on the retracement. And this is best done by switching to the lower time frame (1H) and entering on the breakout. I would really appreciate if you could publish a chart to show me how you do it with your comments. Would you use just fibo or something trickier to define that entry point? If you were to use an Entry Stop where would you place it?  
  
  
  
All you want to know is the substantial part of trading knowledge that is enough to have a decent living with trading, but don’t worry friend, I will publish enough in future, just try to discover in your own because there is a possibility that you find out some tricks that I never could see. I try to send a bit more about them at this weekend.  
  
  
  
  
  
To be continued and thank you again.

Hello,  
  
Thanks for sharing your system! So far it looks great. It combines most of the concepts I've seen in other MA systems. Your charts are very easy to read too.  
  
One thing about the charts. You say that the close price is very important but your red and green bars cover up the close price. Is this because the close price is part of the red/blue calculation? It's possible to show the bars through the histogram, as with the Heiken Ashi MT4 indicator. I can see the problem others mentioned about the timer but I'd call it pretty minor.  
  
I noticed in your document and in your posts you sometimes say "violate" instead of "volatile". I understand why, but it could get confusing ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) The only other problem I had with the document is the blue-on-while text on some pages. I had a hard time reading it.

> One thing about the charts. You say that the close price is very important but your red and green bars cover up the close price.

The close prices are the tiny pins on each bar. On the blue bars it's the top pin, and on the red bars it's the bottom pin.

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

Hello All  
  
  
  
\- My meaning was oscillation, so it was violates and definitely not volatile, anyway it was better to write a better verb and I really had not time to check my text plus I am not a native speaker of English and it is one of 6 languages that I have the acquaintance, either closer or nodding,  
  
Hereafter I will do check and anyway sorry for any misspelling or misleading sentences, please don’t hesitate to remind if there is any wrong, I believe there is no dumb question.  
  
  
  
\- I get many messages, emails requesting more information, specific questions about many aspects, I again tell you please have patience, everything will be better than you can believe it. Most of friends are happy that could find a method that really works, as I saw there are different levels of knowledge among these guys and I have to think to cover the needs of all these different types. So if you read something that is so easy and clear or that is so obscure for you please don’t distress yourself and just never abandon hope, time will come that you will find out what I wanted to mention.  
  
  
  
\- I don’t want to tell that preparing an alarm is not a good idea, just as a member I want to tell my opinion, forex is not a horse race, and it is like a marathon. So you really never be rash, knowing that at what moment the arrow signal gives alarm/appears is not important, because it has its own definition and it never get confirmed before closing the candle, when working H4 chart, you need a check each 4 hour and I will tell you that even you will find out how to estimate when the signal will come, for example yesterday majors rose sharply and many jumped in to trade, I never did, because I know always these is an opportunity to enter after original signal. You never need to catch all signals or the signals at the first moment; you should have a good understanding of the market, currency pairs and timing. I will cover them, so you really don’t need an alarm, I hate alarm, alarm is for emergency things, alarm means stress and stress will destroy your performance; this is not emergency work, it is a job, and it is 24/5, so if you want to make all your life an emergency you are free to do it. Decide which side you are, you are dedicating your life to forex or you are using forex to make your life better?! I was a bit frank of remarking these, it is just my opinions and I do apologize if this makes anybody inconvenient.   
  
  
  
\- Please don’t regard all currency pairs if you can not cover all of them, I recommend follow 2 of them, one major and one minor, for example GBPUSD and EURJPY, after that you will get the correlations between currency pairs. I will explain it too in upcoming weeks.  
  
  
  
\- some of friends are focusing on minor matters, you just try to focus on the great concepts of the markets, like patterns, resistance/supports, pivots, daily/weekly range, momentum, candle patterns and so on. When I say the close price is important you don’t need to know all about the close price and its relations with other aspects, let me simplify the matter, you don’t need monitoring 24/5, you don’t need lots of books, you don’t need the best facilities to trade better, you just need to know a simple way to make winner trades in a long run, we will do it, side by side and this will be happen with patience and perseverance. So when I don’t answer some questions clearly it is because I know you will find out that yourself and better than the way I explain in future after some experience.  
  
  
  
This weekend I will post some about the rest of this method.  
  
  
  
Have a nice day all buds  
  
Ibo

This is part of the knife system and the 8 bars back is the neutral line for the 8sma. I'm not sure on Ibo's thoughts on this as an entry criteria but would be interested to hear from him.  
  
I did not mention the turn of the 8sma in the charts posted, but I would use that as a condition of entry.  
  
I would be interested in an opinion on the other points I have mentioned referencing the distance from the 8 to the 55 SMA as conditions of entry as a a part of the Ibo system.  
Also the validity of the trend line in the EURCHF. Should we wait for a break of this line to enter (Trend lines rule ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) ) This would then bring the 8SMA very near the 55SAM, and from what I uderstand from Ibo's pdf too close is no good as we won't have sufficient pips for a good trade if it retraces off the 55sma.

  * [#40](/thread/post/52173#post52173 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 9:18pm  Apr 19, 2006 6:55pm | Edited 9:18pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Hello friends,  
  
  
  
When I was a child I liked to learn swimming, I tried to do that whenever and wherever I could. I did all the things that swimmers tried to learn me, how to float, how to breath, how to stroke but I scared of water, of getting soaked totally, of death, in fact I did not have the self-confidence, I was thinking there is something else that they did not tell me, there is a secret that I don’t now still, then I focus on minutiae much and much, but no response, no result, still failing to swim, then I told myself that am I ham-handed? The way of my swimming was right but there was something wrong with that, it was the belief that I can do it and I should take the bitter with the sweet. Very similar goes for trading, newbies and struggling traders know whatever that is enough to make money and trade profitably in a long run but they can not do it mostly, because always they are thinking that there is something that they need to know to start trading. I promise you that you will learn more than all your knowledge that ever have learned when you are one day rely on and believe in yourself. **KISS** , the old proverb: Keep It Simple and Stupid; the best systems are the simplest. I learned swimming when I never scared of water and drowning, so if you are scaring of losing and making mistakes then you never learn how to trade.  
  
  
  
I see many like to put themselves in trouble and make money with many struggles, yes, making money is not easy it is a hard work but hard work not impossible.  
  
  
  
I’d like to tell about simplicity and generality, please before reading something about markets look at that how it is general or it is simple, the general matters will waste your time, they give examples without mentioning what security (currency pair/symbol) they are talking, what time frame they are using, they say TREND, but trend means when the time frame has been mentioned. For the sake of simplicity let’s say the daily trend of eurusd is up and on H4 is up but on H1 is down and in M30 and M15 is down and in M5 and M1 is up (the prevailing trend) so it is foolish to tell the trend is up or down without remarking the time scale, and the behavior of symbols are very different, this is why many are professional just in 2/3 symbols and can not trade or at least don’t like trade other so when we say let’s say 20 pips, 8 bars, London Opening and so on, it is very different in each symbol. So this is general and will make you troubles, you will think that you don’t know enough.  
  
  
  
About the performance, you saw the work of MM, I thanked him, they seem excellent, but in real trading you can not get all of them, I call this performance mechanical or psych-free result. In real trading you will get confused and just simple rules will help you. This is not mathematic, nothing is 100% and we are not here to calculate something during the market hour, we are here to recognize and show our art of trading, don’t count pips, don’t count dollars, don’t count your dedicated time to monitor the market, don’t count the amount of your trades. It is not necessary you get in each day or have an open position to feel that you are making money. Most of time standing aside and doing nothing is making you money, because you don’t trade and then you don’t lose money. I was out completely previous week, because there was not any good set up to enter, many entered and lost or I saw they did many trades and at the end of week they had a bunch of winner and loser trades totally fruitless. The pain of a loser trade is more than the equivalent pleasure of a winner trade, so they were not break-even, they felt painfully and this is harmful for health, 1 pip in eurusd is almost 10 dollar in standard accounts but health is priceless.  
  
  
  
I just have published the best entry set up, I will tell many set ups that will enlighten your way to enter in any situation or avoid you to enter.  
  
One important thing need to be mentioned, It is about the amount/percentage of zooming on screen/charts. Please always look at charts sometimes with a good zoom out. You should see the trends, prevailing trends, major support and resistances and the tops and dips. Every day before checking the market look at the daily chart and sometimes weekly chart, I know that at first you can not understand anything from them, but I promise you that in a long term you will find a gut understanding of where price is going and then you will be so clever to find which signal is true or wrong.  
  
  
  
Dear friends please forgive me for being so clear in expressing my opinions, this is not maybe so decent but I really want to say that I never think that I give you rules or want to change your mind, I am just a member like all of you and will feel better if I am a bit of help for you.  
  
  
  
Good trading  
  
Ibo

Some people were talking about EURCHF. I went long based on the simultaneous break of a daily pin bar, pivot and 50 retrace. It's also a Knife trade if you use the pin bar instead of weekly trend direction.  
  
Euro's system shows blue bars so this backs it up. I'm a bit worried about a repeat of the recent downturn which would seem likely to happen just by eyeballing the chart.  
  
Someone mentioned going long on EURGBP. This is why you don't trade into resistance if you look at what happened since then. Set a buy stop on the other side of the MA next time ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f641.png?v=15.1)  
  
GBP seems much stronger than CHF right now (USDCHF looks like a coming reversal), and Euro seems to be weakening, so EURCHF has a good chance I think. The problem is, it's a lot of time to spend on a trade that'll probably make less than 50 pips ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

Sashazz am writing the following based on what i thinking after reading your quote above....please ALL read very carefully.  
  
Our only goal in trading should be to make MONEY. We establish our STYLE, we get a strategy/system that suits that STYLE and we back test the strategy/system to breaking point (on OUR data). We take it apart, put it back together, take it apart again and put it back together. We change this, change that, ask questions, ask more questions. We keep going until we have built incredible confidence in the system/strategy. We never trade a system until we have graded our performance on using the system (in my book, we should score 97% before even thinking about trading real money).  
  
  
  
We always WAIT for the MARKET to come to US. We are not GAMBLERS and should never chase a Setup or the market.   
  
  
  
Am writing the above because I can see some of us have not taken the time to understand or do the required homework on EJ’s 4Hrs method. What’s the difference between EJ’s 4Hr method and Vegas’s 4Hr Method? What were the creators of these strategies thinking? What can they see that we might not be seeing? What is their trading STYLE? When would they trade the strategies or stay out? WHY? Etc….  
  
  
  
Happy Trading  
  
MM

The greatest achievements are those that benefit others....

Sashazz,  
  
I agree with you. I think the Vegas Wealth Builder system has some serious merit, but I found the interpretation of reversal candles, the use of multiple Fib levels based on currency pair and some other items left far too much to the imagination. The EJ model, at first glance, seems more intuitive and simple, though that is just my first impression. Some systems resonate with some traders while others don't. This is just my opinion.  
  
I look forward to learning more about this method with you all in the coming weeks...

Hi Ibo,  
  
Thanks so much for being generous with both your trading method and your willingness to help us all learn more about it. It looks very intriguing, to say the least.   
  
I did have one big question for you. In the introduction to the method in your PDF document, you state: "**When yellow line (55SMA) has a positive slope means the major trend is up and we buy, when pointing down we go short (sell)".** However, later in your EUR/USD trade example, you say "**In this type of entry the slope of yellow must not be regarded except when price is getting closer to that, because it may rebound from that and continue its major trend that would be our exit point."**  
  
What is your rule of thumb in determining whether or not to open a trade when the trading signal is in conflict with the direction of the 55 SMA? Do you just look at a timeframe above the 4H (say Daily) to confirm the trade signal?   
  
Thanks,  
  
Ian

Ian you asked a good question. We don't play with lines/MAs. my meaning of this type of entry was the best entry setup, you should recognize a decent trend then expect a good reversal (good distance between lines), so now you ask what is a decent trend, I have a short answer wait 1 day more and read it tomorrow in EJ_4H Method Part II.  
  
Rgds

> Quoting iboersma
> 
> Disliked
> 
> What is your rule of thumb in determining whether or not to open a trade when the trading signal is in conflict with the direction of the 55 SMA? Do you just look at a timeframe above the 4H (say Daily) to confirm the trade signal?

> Ignored

A common response (from various MA systems I've read about) to the question of when not to trade toward the slow MA is (another question):  
  
Is it possible to tell the difference between a rebound off the slow MA versus a crossing of the MA, and still take some decent profit in the time it takes to react to the bad news?  
  
My definitions for these things include at least 8-12 hours while I might be away from my computer after I think the trade is going well, and/or a well-considered stoploss placement. It's hard to translate price into time, so...  
  
Some systems I've looked at don't consider entering the trade until both the price and fast MA fully cross or bounce off the slow MA, **and then** the price touches the fast MA **and then** starts to move in the desired direction.  
  
There's a lot of stuff to consider, but the stuff about fitting the system to your schedule is really important and is the main mistake I've been making lately. There's some advice floating around about only trading off daily or higher charts, and it makes more and more sense as time goes on. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#63](/thread/post/52787#post52787 "Post Permalink")

  * Apr 21, 2006 3:35pm  Apr 21, 2006 3:35pm 

  * [ Mike Jolley](mike*jolley)

  * | Joined Feb 2006  | Status: Trader | [89 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=6383)

> Quoting sashazz
> 
> Disliked
> 
> I have a question for those of you, why are using MT4: There is a Fibonacci extension tool with the default values 61,8; 100; 161.8  
>    
>  I read somewhere before, and I did it this way: I added extensions to my regular Fibonacci tool, so that it draws retracements and extensions in one go at : 127. 2; 161.8; 2; 261.8. Why would the lines be at different places? And which one you think is correct? See yellow and magenta lines.
> 
> Ignored

Fib levels fall under the category of "probable support and resistance". I like trendlines and actual recent highs and lows better.  
  
The only lines that are correct are the ones you actually see the price reacting to. If several lines happen to be in the same place, one of them might be "correct" but you still need to see how price reacts to this level.  
  
Watch how price reacts to the fib levels. It will tend to bounce around within them. This is more to keep you out of trades than get you in them, which is good. If price crashes through or bounces hard off several fib levels drawn from different points, you might have something. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

I'm playing daily trendline breakouts on this (hmm, it might have just broke upward as I'm writing this) but look at GBPUSD when it first started breaking out on the week of 4/2. It fully reversed, consolidated again, and then actually broke out. So be careful.

  * [#65](/thread/post/52795#post52795 "Post Permalink")

  * Apr 21, 2006 4:33pm  Apr 21, 2006 4:33pm 

  * [ Mike Jolley](mike*jolley)

  * | Joined Feb 2006  | Status: Trader | [89 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=6383)

I don't want to monopolize the conversation, but there's a cool feature of the brightly colored EJ charts if you spread them out in an MT4 profile.  
  
You can easily see which trades are correlated. For example, AUDUSD, EURJPY, EURUSD, and GBPUSD are behaving about the same right now. USDCAD, USDJPY, and USDCHF are all doing pretty much the opposite.  
  
This looks like a good way to quickly judge the overall market and pick only the best pairs to trade while not getting overly invested in a single currency.

> Quoting Lindsay
> 
> Disliked
> 
> There's a lot of stuff to consider, but the stuff about fitting the system to your schedule is really important and is the main mistake I've been making lately. There's some advice floating around about only trading off daily or higher charts, and it makes more and more sense as time goes on.
> 
> Ignored

**I keep thinking about the higher time frames too. I can see direct benefit in trading the daily at least. but what stops me is the kinds of stop loss and trade management needed for these time frame. I expect you would need some pretty big "Kahoona's" or wallet to trade effectively**[/quote]  
  
Lindsay,  
  
I agree. Trading the higher timeframes (daily and above) is a luxury that many of us "little guys/gals" can't really afford without significant capital to enable us to absorb the inevitably higher drawdowns. Whipsawing at this level takes on a whole new meaning and really tests your psychological trading mettle. That's why I think the 4H timeframe is a happy medium between the 1H and the daily. You can easily see the trend on that level, but your range/whipsawing generally isn't astronomical.   
  
I use the Daily timeframe to confirm my trades at lower timeframes, but have had little success trading solely at that timeframe... Just my two cents on the issue. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1)  
  
Ian

> Quoting Mike Jolley
> 
> Disliked
> 
> A common response (from various MA systems I've read about) to the question of when not to trade toward the slow MA is (another question):  
>    
>  Is it possible to tell the difference between a rebound off the slow MA versus a crossing of the MA, and still take some decent profit in the time it takes to react to the bad news?  
>    
>  My definitions for these things include at least 8-12 hours while I might be away from my computer after I think the trade is going well, and/or a well-considered stoploss placement. It's hard to translate price into time, so...  
>    
>  Some systems I've looked at don't consider entering the trade until both the price and fast MA fully cross or bounce off the slow MA, **and then** the price touches the fast MA **and then** starts to move in the desired direction.  
>    
>  There's a lot of stuff to consider, but the stuff about fitting the system to your schedule is really important and is the main mistake I've been making lately. There's some advice floating around about only trading off daily or higher charts, and it makes more and more sense as time goes on.
> 
> Ignored

Thanks for your insight, Mike. I think the issue with many of the systems I've seen that require a touch of the slow/fast MAs is that you have given up a significant portion of pips waiting for it to happen. I'm all for being conservative in Forex and waiting for multiple confirmations before entering a trade, but I'm not convinced that the touch/bounce MA systems are any more reliable than the "slope change"/bar color change systems like the EJ-4H and the like.  
  
I also agree that trading on the daily and higher timeframes would be great - the trend is unmistakeable and gives you much more confidence in your trade - the downside is the fact that you need far more capital to absorb the greater drawdown and nerves of steel to wait out the big swings in price.  
  
Like you, I also think Ibo's colored bars are one of the coolest additions to the MT4 charts I've seen. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

  * [#90](/thread/post/53109#post53109 "Post Permalink")

  * Apr 23, 2006 10:03am  Apr 23, 2006 10:03am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar5364_4.gif) Lindsay](lindsay)

  * | Joined Jan 2006  | Status: Aussie Battler | [64 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=5364)

I have been looking at the 34EMA as a stop placement when in a trade. If price closes above the 34 when selling or below when in a buy I would then exit the trade. I have manually backtested this and compared the results to getting out on a turn of the 8ma or a 30, 40, 50 pip trailing stop and have found that even though it gets a little scary some times I get far better rides sticking to the close above or below the 34 EMA.  
The areas where price consolidates or retraces a long move I would normally get stopped out and miss some good moves. With the 34 ema even though you give back some pips sometimes it still I beleive gives better overall results.  
Also I entered the USDCHF and USDJPY for buys from their most recent buy signals on the 20th of April and now looking at my 34 ema theory realise I should have stayed out. I'm not saying that to enter a trade that their should aways be across over the 34 ema it would to often give up too many pips. On the other hand it may be beneficial where there has been a long move waiting for price to cross the 34 to get out and sometimes to get in.  
I would really love some others to back test my theory and compare their own results on getting out on the price closing above or below the 34 EMA. I realise that my doing it manually can be subject to errors and subconcious bias. 

Attached Image

![](/attachment/image/4775?d=1145754135)

It was in the Private Forum but I was since posted somewhere in the FF, I looked but could not find where.  
The emas are 55 and 8 and the dotted lines are fib levels off the 55 ma showing possible overbought and oversold areas. You can adjust the fib levels in the properties box to either 1,2 or 3 depending upon the currencies tendencies and visually where price sits on the fibs most often.

  * [#97](/thread/post/53141#post53141 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited Apr 24, 2006 3:39am  Apr 23, 2006 3:22pm | Edited Apr 24, 2006 3:39am 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Hello Kids,  
  
1- Read the first post again for instructions (this may help some newbies that have problems in setting up the method)  
  
2- PROPER ENTRY: this is what we will work at least 6 months to find out how to enter properly.  
  
3- About discussing trades by this method I agree, maybe this will help you to get closer to the method, but don't start another thread please, this may diversify the efforts.  
  
4- I will cover how to trail the price, how to book your profits, how to manage your account and positions, how to minimize the risk, but friends all these will take its proper time, so don't hurry, I do not expect that you trade excellent at this time by this method, just if you use the best entry setup you are the best student.  
  
5- You should keep it simple, don't try to enter more indicators to support some aspects, all aspects that you can not find at the time being, will be discussed in future.  
  
6- Please forget pips/day, at least say pips/week. With this mehtod you are aiming intellectual targets like 100 pips, so don't think that you can seize 20 pips per day, try to trade one time a week but profitably and with less stress., expend the rest of your time to enjoy the life. If you can make 100 pips consistently per week I will show you that you will be a millionaire just in 2 years. So don't try to make more and more with working 24/7. This is not the way.  
  
7- The methos of 34 EMA is working on M30 chart so please read number 9 below.  
  
8- If you find or think of something usefull with this method (like indicators, tricks, templates and so on) before posting, please send me a private email describing your opinion and I will try it before publishing to avoid wasting the time of kids and perturbing their learning.  
  
9- If you want that I shorten your way to win at least one year just please bear in mind that :  
  
A)All indicators in MT4 and most of custom indicators are useless, just some of them with their special setting are a bit of help; so don't waste your time to discover a magic from them. I just like Ichimoku because it is really predict the potential supports/resistances.  
  
B)Don't strive to trade smaller time frame than H4.  
  
All these were my personal opinions, I am maybe mistaken, I just told my own oipnions with all respects.  
  
Happy trading  
Ibo

Hi ForexMike,  
  
As far as setting up the charts to look the way Ibo has them, I didn't fiddle with adding this indicator here or that one there, I just overlaid the appropriate template onto my chart. If you added Ibo's indicators and compiled them before overlaying the template, it should automatically add the correct indicators. If you find you want to add or remove one or more, you can do so at that point, but just adding the template to the chart should do the trick for most of what you need.   
  
Hope this helps,  
  
Ian

Ibo,  
  
**From a sheer technical point of view** , it looks like the USD bulls may be in line to take another run at buying up the dollar on Monday. EUR/USD and GBP/USD both show as overbought in the 4H and Daily stochastics and the price action looks to be retracing downward again. Same situation for the other USD pairs.   
  
**Fundamentally, however,** given that the interest-rate differential of the USD is steadily waning, that several countries (including Switzerland most recently) are divesting themselves of the dollar as the primary denomination of their currency reserves, and that the general macroeconomic health of the US seems to be less assured every day, I wonder how long even minor USD bullishness can last. The overriding trend is definitely bearish the dollar in my opinion.   
  
Ibo - What is your view on using technicals vs. fundamentals with the EJ_4H method? Do you integrate fundamentals within your trading or do you just let the price action dictate your trades 100%? What about big news releases - do you close out of your positions beforehand or just ride the storm?  
  
Thanks in advance,  
  
Ian

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

Dear Traders,  
  
Fundamental aspects will be covered on time, at the time shortly I should tell you that forget them totally, Just for some being preserved don't enter a trade if there is a very important news on the way to be aired or take a very preserving risk management if you have some positions on.  
  
I have a suggestion about discussing daily trading oportunities or comments or forecast, I think it is better that if any member like to talk about such issues color-code it by dark blue (or another common agreed color)  
  
I see that many of kids are so eager to talk about taking positions and talking about them, I took gbp and audusd (short) and booked them with 0 and -15 pips, still gbp and eur has lower sentiment but this is business and price is king, I prefered to wait and see what is the price action on Monday. So your short trades on eur and gbp were right decisions, you have gotten right direction, but there are many times that market completely act contrary to the consensus.  
  
Rgds  
Ibo

  * [#119](/thread/post/53459#post53459 "Post Permalink")

  * Apr 25, 2006 5:19pm  Apr 25, 2006 5:19pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Hi everybody,  
  
bigballer thanks for your suggestion, but as most of members were agreed with me, we preferably never start another group. I am sure this work will just distract us especially new members.  
  
I have received many emails demanding a signal sending service, friends, I know that there are many sites related to known associations/brokers that offer forex learning up to 2k and at least $500 and give you just some fruitless documents of very old indicators and general rules. I know that they offer you indicators that never has a good performance for hundreds of dollars. I am thinking about this matter that provide a signal service that needs an update just one time each 24hr. If I made a solid decision I will tell you in advance, but I think it will take time. At that service I should provide an online sessions to tell very detailed tricks. When I use tricks, it is not a secret, it is all about what all traders have in hand but some can filter the misleading aspect and extract proper views and some can not.   
  
Still I am not sure that I will discuss at all about the current situation of the market and opportunities or not. I afraid that this may not help you and harm your self-confidence, but I know that you should have trainers/teachers for all your life's aspects.  
  
If you have any discussion about this matter, please send me a message or a private email.  
  
Happy trading  
Ibo

I think it would be nice for Ibo to take us through a trade or two but i don't think this will help anyone (really). We are traders and Ibo has given us a good tool to trade with. It is now down to each one to adapt this tool to their trading style. Ibo's trading style is very different to mine and am sure it is very different to yours. Discussing what we see/don't see on a chart will be great but walking people through trades.......NO NO.

Well, based on this system I personally don't agree with this trade for the following 3 reasons:  
1.There is no space between the price and the 55EMA  
2.The 55EMA is a very very strong downtrend, which means that it's not that wise to enter a long position.  
3.Both long-term and short-term Stochastic Oscillators are in overbought area.  
  
I might rather wait for a rebound from the 55EMA and enter a short trade instead.  
  
Happy trading and welcome to forex.

I like the look of a possible long trade. I think that I would wait for a close above the 50% retracement of the prior high at 115.95 and the recent low. The pair have consolidated after a lengthy move down and the consolidation may well prove to be exhaustion. Retracing a long move is to be expected and the 50% area may be a strong resistance level and lead to a further downturn, that is why I would wait for a close above the 50% retracement

Hi Snags,  
  
I entered the same long USD/JPY trade you did at 114.98 and am still riding it at the current price of 115.18. USD/JPY took a serious drop and a correction is due. The 5-period stoch was nearing overbought when I went long, but we all know that can last as overbought for a while. In addition, the 30-period stoch is a far better indicator of potential for direction, and it was reading 6, which is in-line with value at the beginning of other corrections in the pair. I set my take-profit to 115.47 as I based it on possible resistance created from the daily low of 115.50, set on 03/20. Nevertheless, I'm keeping a close eye on the price, as I'm not convinced this pair has the momentum to even approach that resistance at this point...  
  
Yes, the 55SMA is heading down, but in my opinion, that's to be expected with the significant drop the pair took when it gapped down.   
  
I would like to hear Ibo's opinion on this trade as well, but I think it is in-line with the EJ_4H method rules.  
  
Keep in mind that Ibo wants us all to enter our trading comments in _**BLUE**_ so they can be differentiated from his. This will make it easier for newbies to the thread to quickly review Ibo's entries from the rest of ours if they don't want to read all the banter right off the bat.   
  
Happy trading,  
  
Ian![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

> Well, based on this system I personally don't agree with this trade for the following 3 reasons:

>  Happy trading and welcome to forex.

Rongshishong,  
  
I'm not sure what you mean when you say there's "no space between the price and the 55EMA". When I bought (and roughly when Snag bought), the price was at 114.98 and the 55EMA was at 117.03, making the difference 203 pips, which is more space than this pair has seen for quite a while...  
  
Yes, the 55EMA is moving down sharply, but because the pair gapped down so severely, I would hesitate to call this a true "downtrend" of any length as that is not confirmed on the Daily chart, so I personally ignored the slope of the 55EMA for this trade.  
  
My short-term Stoch was nearing overbought when I went long, but the long-term was at rock bottom (which is a far better indicator of overall direction than the short), so I'm confused as to what long-term Stoch you were reading.  
  
Take a look at 12/19/2005 on USD/JPY and you'll see a similar trading setup to the one we see today, which was good for around 100 pips.  
  
\- Ian

Dear All   
  
Sorry for delay, I had a problem in connecting to the net and could not send promised issue on time.  
  
Stop Loss Placing although is a very important thing and there are several ways to do this but most of the time traders use a very simple and easy to place regarding some aspects that I will discuss later on. You can find out how you should place a surefire stop for an entry, you get 5-20 pips regarding your risk-reward ratio and the currency pair and some other aspects like the volatility the market and relations with PPs and fibo levels. It is not important that at the time you can get the best entry, everybody will have problems and mistakes in starting. please consider that YOU WILL LEARN WHEN YOU MAKE A MISTAKE. so if you are making mistakes don't distress yourself, just please refer to that and learn ONE THING from that, after some time you get better and better and at that time you have not much mistakes and then you will try for higher performances.  
  
Thanks all kids sent some stuff.

TimeFreedom,  
  
You said the thing that I will tell in upcoming psychologic issues frequently, many learn how to trade but few learn how not to trade; there are some conditions that you should feel and stand aside, just be patient and wait for the best. 1 trade each week is enough, don't imagine that 100 pips is few. You should never think of the number of trades, the number of pips, you should think about performance. After months of experience I found out that the key to success is recognizing when to trade and when staying out even you have a very strong strategy/system.  
  
Rgds,

Timefreedom  
  
There are three actions that you will ask yourself on a daily basis as a trader: 1) Am i Buying? 2) Am i Selling? and 3) Should i Stand aside? The most difficult for most traders is number 3. Number 1&2 require you to have a good strategy/system and to be disciplined enough to pull the trigger when you get a trading signal. Number 3 requires a great deal of 'Personal' discipline. You have to know how to wait for the right trades, you have to know how to wait for the market to show you where it is going and you need to have tremendous mental strength.   
  
Use your pain of loss to turn yourself into a better trader. Keeping records of your trades is a good starting point to developing the good discipline required to be a great trader.  
  
Happy Trading  
MM![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f44d.png?v=15.1)   
  
**Ps. NEVER forget to place your stop losses.**

The greatest achievements are those that benefit others....

Ishay,  
  
Don't despair. Many download MetaTrader and use a demo price feed to do their analysis and then make their trades with their broker, using their proprietary platform. It is much more convenient to have MT4 be your trading platform when using systems like EJ_4H, but it's not the end of the world if you don't.  
  
Happy trading,  
  
Ian

1-please don’t forget the blue color of texts discussing about positions and daily market.  
  
  
  
2-Traders who use other platforms can register for a demo account of a broker who uses MT4 as its platform, up the method’s implements in the MT4 and trade on their platforms when their MT4 gives a signal that suits them.  
  
  
  
3- Regarding many requests from members it is likely that I construct a private mentoring service, of course this will be limited in case of getting assured. (I think it will be 10 members totally). I am designing a very different and proper mentoring program for both newbies and struggling traders. This may be a very new method in mentoring focusing on personal abilities and experiences of the members. A pretest may be taken to recognition of the level and characteristics and needs of the member. More detailed in upcoming weeks. The free document parts will be OK but the private members will have premiums and some detailed information that won’t be discussed in that documents.

  * May 2, 2006 1:00am  May 2, 2006 1:00am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar8826_5.gif) skyline](skyline)

  * Joined Apr 2006 | Status: Metatrader Programmer | [1,417 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=8826)

I backtested manually on some pairs using EJ method applying a starting/closing trade on next bar that is opened after one was closed with an arrow.   
Here's some results:  
  
**AUD/JPY - March 2006**  
short 87.05 out 86.30 = +75 pips  
long 86.30 tp 87.08 = +78 pips   
short 87.08 tp 86.89 = +19 pips  
long 86.89 out 86.46 = -43 pips  
short 86.46 tp 83.96 = +250 pips  
short 83.91 tp 82.74 = +117 pips  
long 82.74 tp 84.07 = +133 pips  
total : +629 pips  
  
**USD/CAD - March 2006**  
long 1.1332 tp 1.1614 = +282 pips  
short 1.1614 tp 1.1579 = +35 pips  
long 1.1579 tp 1.1663 = +84 pips  
short 1.1663 out 1.1685 = -22 pips  
long 1.1685 out 1.1672 = -13 pips  
short 1.1672 out 1.1689 = -17 pips  
long 1.1689 out 1.1711 = +22 pips   
short 1.1711 out 1.1663 = +48 pips  
total : +419 pips  
  
**GBP/CHF - March 2006**  
short 2.2994 tp 2.2723 = +271 pips  
long 2.2723 tp 2.2751 = +28 pips  
short 2.2751 out 2.2785 = -34 pips  
long 2.2785 out 2.2743 = -42 pips  
short 2.2743 tp 2.2631 = +112 pips  
long 2.2631 tp 2.2698 = +67 pips  
short 2.2698 out 2.2723 = -25 pips   
long 2.2723 tp 2.2794 = +71 pips  
short 2.2794 tp 2.2640 = +154 pips  
total : +602 pips  
  
**EUR/JPY - March 2006**  
long 138.08 tp 140.20 = +212 pips  
short 140.20 out 140.36 = -16 pips  
long 140.36 tp 141.74 = +138 pips  
short 141.74 tp 141.54 = +20 pips  
long 141.54 tp 141.82 = +28 pips  
short 141.82 tp 141.20 = +62 pips  
long 141.20 tp 141.37 = +17 pips  
short 141.37 tp 141.31 = +6 pips  
long 141.31 out 140.66 = -65 pips  
short 140.66 out 141.11 = -45 pips  
long 141.11 tp 143.96 = +285 pips  
total : +642 pips  
  
Everyone can check and it seems that only few trade will be closed with low pips loss, while most of trades are in huge profit as you can verify by yourself.

Hi Ibo,  
  
It would seem to me that the EJ_4H method is purposely built to take advantage of reversals in a ranging/lightly trending market. **Given that all signs point to the beginning of what could be longer-term overall weakness in the USD across most currencies, we may find ourselves in a heavily trending market.** Yes, there will some retracements that we can take advantage of, but in a heavily trending market, the price rarely crosses the 55SMA, but more often bounces off of it. _Given that you DO NOT advise entering a long trade when the 8SMA is ABOVE the 55SMA (and vice-versa for SHORT trades), it would seem to me that we would be looking at very, very few "acceptable" trades using this method within a seriously trending market._   
  
Take a look at EUR/USD on the 4H chart from November, 2003 to January, 2004 or you can look at EUR/USD from October, 2004 to December, 2004. During these two time periods, the EUR was on a serious roll and we had, perhaps, 2 to 3 trade possibilities that met all the criteria for the EJ_4H method (e.g.: 8SMA below 55SMA and moving up, sufficient distance between 8SMA and 55SMA, etc.) Not being a trend trader myself, I'm hoping this same trendedness doesn't take over all the USD pairs, but I'm also a realist, and it looks like that well may happen.   
  
How do you reconcile the current trending market conditions with the EJ_4H method? Is there any room to enter long trades even though the 8SMA is ABOVE the 55SMA (since I don't anticipate seeing the 8SMA cross below the 55SMA that often)? If not, we may see little return using this method on USD pairs as we will not have many trading signals. and may have to just trade the crosses.  
  
Thoughts?  
  
\- Ian

Could you post your EA Robik? So i can try to adapt to my trading style to EJ ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1)  
I used H4 timeframe and only arrows. Furthermore my backtest was only manual so there was no stop loss , but simply i write down entry and exit value, so i have a short position then a long , then again a short and so on. It's quite simple to do this in EJ method 'cause there is arrows that tell us when to enter and exit from trade. Obviously when i'm a actual trade i put a large stop loss (about 100 pips) and adjust trailing when i hit important pips gain.   
However using this mechanical way to trade EJ method, since last 27 Apr i have 7 positions opened for a total of about 800-900 pips (just today i closed one position on gbp/jpy because trailing stop of 100 pips was reached in a retrace).  
  
![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f44d.png?v=15.1)

Dear Ian and all friends,  
  
  
  
Thanks for your notes, it is good to mention and strive to discover the reality of everything.  
  
  
  
1- Again you are rash, I just told the best entry setup, as you mentioned this is a reversal trading method and there are many setups that let you enter a position. On the other hand we have many securities to trade, moreover we are here to make money, it is not important that you trade EUR or GBP or Gold or any other symbol. Remember that I told you should get familiar with behavior of pairs. Majors totally are so skittish and volatile as well as forex is a very sensitive market.  
  
2- I can not really learn all you need by this way, because everybody has his/her own demands and level, so this needs a proper private mentoring and following market for some month to see how we should act in any situation and get stronger to implement the method for ourselves.  
  
3- If there is somebody who tells can learn a strong method to you just in a very short period I think he/she is maybe an imposter. I guess I need to publish at least 20 parts of my documents to reveal sufficient aspects of method to trade properly and profitably. Maybe at the time you are making money just with this few data, but my meaning of properly was so complex, some methods and most of time short term methods is so harmful to health. You will find out when it is late. Health is priceless.   
  
4- If you just enter arrow signals in long run you will be winner but why in practice guys can not do this? It is because they neglect the emotion, stress, patience, daily news or rumors airing pressures, commentaries. Because they neglect proper risk management with the method. Because they are living in many different time zones and miss some opportunities, because they have different personality and lifestyle. I can enumerate more.  
  
5- If this really works, why free, why I did not sell it? Making money is a need but until your income meets your needs, more than that will hurt you. Personally I like art of trading and when I see that I can make money when I want then I don’t have any desire to strive for more and more. We had many millionaire traders or maybe billionaire, but we have just one trader named W. D. Gann. I never want to say that I want to be famous; it is really never help me to be happy man. I feel I am happy really when I see that I am a bit of help for others. So, I have to differentiate between people who want to know much and appreciate and who just want to be a second-guesser.   
  
6- Last but not least, all our methods are on the basis of trending principles so definitely all methods work on the basis of trending markets (supply and demand)  
  
7- It is not so wise that you think you should trade all heavy trends because they are the ones you had to choose. There will be many like this that you will be in doubt to enter or not and when you are in doubt then stay out. The same goes for candles, when you see a candle with 100 pips of range you think that you could seize at least 70 pips of that just in 1 hour easily; but really they are ones you may be so careful to trade (Although in this method I have setups that seize them )  
  
8- I will explain the way to recognize very heavy and strong trends. But this is impossible by this way. It will be possible for private members in conjunction with market following for some months to see different situations of market and being ready for reversals or staying out in time and enjoying their life.  
  
9- I attached 2 snaps to see how it was really so simple 1-2-3 pattern to enter with a breakout confirmation and manage your position, I believe all this trades were aggressive.   
  
  
  
Sorry for long letter,  
  
Good trading  
  
Ibo

I wanted to respond to the EUR/USD Trade and bring to light the USD/CHF pair as well. As the USD/CHF continued to decline, the EUR/USD continued to rise. We effectively have a cross over of the two pairs and research indicates that when this occurs we could see a move.  
  
  
As of right now according to the EJ method, I do see a reversal arrow on both those pairs. EUR/USD pointing down and crossing the 8SMA, and the USD/CHF point up and crossing the 8SMA.  
  
  
**IBO,** I think you make reference in your notes that it may be best to wait for at least two bars to cross over the line before entry to confirm the reversal.  
  
  
Also, I have a hypothetical question: Lets say I were to enter into a short trade of the EUR/USD pair. Price is currently 1.2567. The long term Stoch is at 94, but the short term Stoch is at 10. For a better entry would it be best to wait for that Short term Stoch to rise up before shorting?   
  
  
  
Thanks  
  
Mike

Eacj strategy needs a proper timing, you need just utmost 3/4 checks during day and even can manage positions very professionally than this and update one time each day. This is final goal that I guess private members can reach in a year.  
  
Happy trading,

I was confused about this previously, as your PDF #1 states that going LONG with the 8SMA above the 55SMA is not worth the risk... As you said, nothing is for sure in Forex and much depends on the trader's experience, the tone of the market, etc. so these types of trades must be evaluated within the broader context of the financial instrument.

iboersma,  
  
Little by little I will explain the setups/triggers and other instruments that we should use to enter a position,we just started with the best entry setup to have a good starting and it has its own conditions. Other setups also have their own characteristics and surely instruments to be recognized. remember that I told price is the best indicator. firstly I told use 8/55SMA and candl colors and so on to get a signal then enter a trade. Afterward I explained how to use chart patterns or dual Stoch to get ready and enter with posing orders; I will make it more explicit in weeks,you will see that in last steps you will use the best setup just as a prompt being ready signal or a confirmation for a confluence of signals and events. I believe that lessons for public especially in such issues (trading) is not so effective, because we neglect knowledge, psychological aspects and many factors that I can not discuss here in advance. Again I repeat that as you see this is enough for you to make money, but if you want to be a very powerful professional in trading you should try hard and much. I want to design a plan to help members design their own methods using their personality and condition, so they will be powerful persons that can trade and get adapted to any market. If somebody claim that he/she can do this by pubic lessons I guess it is not fair.  
  
About private mentoring, it is not still 100%, you should keep in mind that this is very strict work and should be regarded carefully. It won't be a forum as I told it is impossible to help traders with same treatment. Each person should do his/her own exercises and the help is completely fitted to his/her level and knowledge. There will be a pretest and a questionnaire to get familiar with the member. Some questions may be asked extraordinary. The instrument mostly will be emailing or maybe chatting in case of being necessary.  
  
Yours,  
Ibo

  * [ ForexMike](forexmike)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [77 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4310)

IBO,  
  
Your thoughts:  
  
Last evening it appears we had reversal on the EUR/USD. Two red arrows appeared and were below the 8SMA. The overall trend is up here.  
  
I took a short was stopped out as the price subsequently raced to new highs. I noticed a blue arrow this morning, but that is now gone.   
  
Would you have taken that trade…? Since the trend was up on the weekly chart would you look only to go long? Or would you primarily look at current price movements?  
  
Thoughts appreciated.

> Quoting eurusdtrader
> 
> Disliked
> 
> **This is a forex trading system on H4 chart with attached indicators and templates.**
> 
>   
>    
>    
>    
>  **Instructions:**  
>    
>  1- You should use MT4.  
>    
>  2- You should Update Monthly, Weekly, Daily, H4, H1 charts when using.  
>    
>  3- You should copy the indicators in .../Meta Trader/experts/indicators folder.  
>    
>  4- You should copy the indicators in .../Meta Trader/templates folder.  
>    
>  5- As this is an easy-to-use method you just use templates to do every thing with this method.(e.g. ususally setup ej_4h for monitoring and when you are predicting market by pivots you setup ej_4h_wp or/and ej_4h_mp and after your calculation back to ej_4h to see the chart with less difficulty.  
>    
>  6- Templates with the extention of "wb" are ones with White Background to facilitate preparing a picture for printing or other use.  
>    
>  **_Abbreviations:_**  
>    
>  ej_4h ------------------------ Basic template (setup)  
>  ej_4h_wp -------------------- Basic setup+weekly pivots  
>  ej_4h_mp -------------------- Basic setup+monthly pivots  
>  ej_4h_dual stoch ------------- Basic setup+dual stochastic oscillator  
>    
>    
>  **_Important Notes:_**  
>    
>    
>  **1- All Updates of indicators, templates and documents will be done in this post (the first #1), just a notification will be sent as a new reply (post).**  
>    
>    
>  **2-The texts/posts in blue color are the ones that members discuss daily/current price action, forecasts and commentaries; so for shortening the duration of following the thread if you are new to thread you can neglect them for awhile. ( We do this not to distract or diversify the efforts of members by starting a new thread, so please be aware that no new thread related to this method should be started)**
> 
> Ignored

> Ignored

OK folks,  
  
In order to set up MT4 to work with the EJ_4H system, you need to:  
  
1) Download ALL indicators, place them in your "Indicators" folder.  
2) Open up each and every one of the indicators you downloaded via the MetaEditor (exclamation mark icon in top menu bar) in MT4. Save and compile each. _This is key as they will not work unless you compile them._  
3) Download all templates and put them in your main "Templates" folder.  
4) Open up the currency charts you want to look at.  
5) In each chart, go to the menu bar at the top of MT4 and click the "Charts" menu. From their select "Templates". You should see the EJ_4H templates you downloaded there. If not, select "Load Template" from the context menu and search for them.  
6) Once you select the template you want (e.g.: EJ_4H_Dual_Stoch, etc.) the chart will change to show the colored bars and other indicator-related information.   
  
If you don't see some of the indicators, like the 4H countdown timer, go to the Indicators icon (green plus sign) on the top menu bar and then select the indicator you want to add.   
  
Much of the confusion about this lies with the fact that people don't realize that the indicators are loaded WITH the template.   
  
Hope this helps,  
  
Ian

i assuming you are trying to put fibo lines around 55 SMA here, right? i was trying to do the same on my other charts, too, and just ended up using envelopes instead. but according with what Ibo teaches, he wants us to use different targets in his system.  
  
my understanding is that if you want to really get into the creator's vision, it is better to use a complete set of his recommendations. i found recently in one of the books about forex: first, you have to learn the rules, then you have to play by the rules, then you have to win by the rules, and only after that you can change the rules. although, myself i am always starting with breaking the rules and very often paying the price for that.

H2M,  
  
This is outlined in the pdf. When I was first starting out in FX, I was constantly looking for indicators and others to place my SL's and TP's. (I'm not indicating that you are doing this but many typically look in this direction)  
  
In the guide, he outlines where to put the stops and gives a generous listing of ideas to use for profits such as fibos, wp's/mp's, trendline direction, etc.  
  
Maybe this will be of enrichment for some.  
  
Cheers to all,  
  
K  
  
P.s. Please take a look at the Eur/Usd (or others) with the 'WP Template' and zoom out a bit. On the EUR/USD, you'll see lots of activity (various resistance/support) around the pivot and midpivot 3. When a "correction" comes, I'd 1st look at the pivot as a TP and then on down.

  * [ ktrade](ktrade)

Mind you pivots change all the time as well as fibos. See now if you were to put a fib on the EUR/USD from the 4/14 move, you'll see the 38 retracement is sitting beautifully on S1. This is another great location to keep an eye on.   
  
Of course this all provided that there isn't a major increase in the pair. (Although there will be most likely another great area such as this one is presenting)  
  
And don't forget to keep an eye on the price retracement levels back to the 55MA.  
  
Cheers,  
  
K

You don't need to monitor the price, you should find a good point to place your orders, reversal is about the majors. Still momentum is high and as you are hearing form media and some professionals some moves of the price is out of phase (non-technical without any solid reason), I personally am waiting for backing to the harmony. This on the basis of my thoughts is happen Saturday, so as that is off then we may have the reversal Friday or Monday. But nothing is 100%. Let's see.  
  
Our method is on H4, for controling your account at the time you should eye H4 chart, but for better entry or exit in the hours that momentum (speed) of price is high you can go down to H1 and do precisely what you need.

  * May 6, 2006 8:28pm  May 6, 2006 8:28pm 

  * [ Ishaypesok](ishaypesok)

  * | Joined Apr 2006  | Status: Trader | [18 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=9190)

[quote=iboersma]OK folks,  
  
In order to set up MT4 to work with the EJ_4H system, you need to:  
  
1) Download ALL indicators, place them in your "Indicators" folder.  
2) Open up each and every one of the indicators you downloaded via the MetaEditor (exclamation mark icon in top menu bar) in MT4. Save and compile each. _This is key as they will not work unless you compile them._  
3) Download all templates and put them in your main "Templates" folder.  
4) Open up the currency charts you want to look at.  
5) In each chart, go to the menu bar at the top of MT4 and click the "Charts" menu. From their select "Templates". You should see the EJ_4H templates you downloaded there. If not, select "Load Template" from the context menu and search for them.  
6) Once you select the template you want (e.g.: EJ_4H_Dual_Stoch, etc.) the chart will change to show the colored bars and other indicator-related information.   
  
If you don't see some of the indicators, like the 4H countdown timer, go to the Indicators icon (green plus sign) on the top menu bar and then select the indicator you want to add.   
  
Much of the confusion about this lies with the fact that people don't realize that the indicators are loaded WITH the template.   
  
Hope this helps,  
  
Ian[/QUOTE  
  
  
Thanks for the most informative reply which answers my queries very nicely.   
  
  
Regards,

  * May 7, 2006 6:49am  May 7, 2006 6:49am 

  * [ ForexMike](forexmike)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [77 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4310)

IBO,  
  
  
  
Looking for an opportunity to learn from your analysis, so I attached a chart of the EUR/JPY and would like your feedback.  
  
  
The weekly trend on this pair is up; however, we had a major down trend in price on Friday. One can clearly see on the attached chart that the price blew through 8SMA (white line) as well as the support level 1, but it did not break support level 2. I missed this opportunity.  
  
  
The 55SMA which shows the main sentiment of the market still shows a slight bias to the upside, but is flattening. The price is now around the 55SMA. Regradless of the fact that the weekly trend is up, the 8 SMA is now sloping downward with a negative bias.  
  
  
If I understand your method correctly, I would be looking for an opportunity to go short, however, we are at the 55SMA and the support level 2 is not that far off.  
  
  
I do not really see a good opportunity here. If I see a green buy arrow (which we might if the price bounces off of the 55 or 2nd support level and retraces) I would not take the trade due to the fact that the risk reward it too great. The 8SMA is still above the 55SMA.  
  
  
According to your method, I really see two primary trade signals.**  
**  
  
**Primary Long: 8SMA is Below 55SMA:** Look for slope to turn positive and you get a green arrow  
  
**Primary Short: 8SMA is ABOVE 55SMA:** Look for slope to turn negative and look for a red arrow.   
  
In an situation where the **8SMA is ABOVE 55SMA**(in the case of a long trade) and the trend is up would you look to buy on recent pullbacks? Perhaps not as a primary trade, but perhaps a secondary with a lower trade size? One may miss the initial primary trade signal and although the 8 has crossed the 55, there could still be considerable upside if the trend is in that direction. Would you agree?   
  
I am wondering if you can outline your primary and secondary (if applicable) trade signals again.   
  
Thoughts on this and/or additional analysis techniques welcome and appreciated.  Mike

Attached Image

IBO,  
  
A follow-up to my last message. This is a view of the EUR/USD 4-hour chart.A nice uptrend is evident. In the chart I drew attention to the most recent blew buy signal arrow. Although the 8SMA is above the 55SMA, would a long trade be entered here.  
  
I also follow the Vegas Wealth Building system, and this pair is trading at it most extreme fib level and keeping an eye at a potential reversal of the trend.  
  
Looking at the most recent trading price, one could make the argument that the trend will continue, and why not jump in and go long? Using the pivot points as a means of additional analysis, the first resistance level (R1) appears to me the major resistance level on both the daily and weekly charts.  
  
Any thoughts here...  
  
Thanks

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

ForexMike,  
About EURJPY chart : Lots of issues needs to be discussed.  
1- I will do the same exercises for private members, in fact they do like you and we will discuss.  
2- I just tell you some that hope will help.   
  
\- A long range candle often means non-technical market, or a vey important news or rumour and so on. Simply, stand aside.  
\- Mondays and Fridays as the starting and finishing of the weekly business round are a little different form the rest. In fact they have its own characteristics. Shortly, Stand aside Mondays and look for a breakout/down at the end of session (most of time eauropean)  
\- You were right about the majority of your talk. But Preferably you should get the direction by two stop orders (buy and sell)  
\- At the time completely forget about the weekly trend, because it is very long time scale  
  
About EURUSD: One very simple but important rule, when you expect a reversal (I see as VWB here that all of kids look for) and it does not happen it means the trend is very strong and you should follow the trend. I will discuss in detail in the future.   
  
Have a nice weekend  
Ibo

I have to add when we are in such situations (expecting reversal never happen and the trend continues) the best strategy to trade is to focus on day trading skills. I won't talk about this skills in this thread or in my documents beause it is not included.Just I will discuss with private members on the basis of need-to-know. So it depends on your ability to seize enough pips when you know the direction and this matter that the tred is strong enough. This is one of the easiest set-ups that you can trade. because price trends with daily steps. You should just take the daily projections.  
  
In fact this is the only condition that you can rely on daytrading and trend following dasics.  
  
  
Yours,  
Ibo

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar1517_4.gif) bigballer](bigballer)

  * | Joined Jan 2005  | Status: Trader | [139 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=1517)

Dear Friends,  
  
As you see in majors we are in the zone that price violates drastically and there are many misleading signals, this is because at the time price is errant and it should go higher or lower to confirm the direstion, as we are expecting the sell-off market eur should break through 1.2260 to confirm the reversal, otherwise we get assured that the uptrend is very strong. Untill now the reversal of Saturday (Monday) that I talk about is going to be confirmed.  
There are methods that we can recognize this zone, it is done using fibo and PP and some other patterns. Will be covered some in future and completely for private members.   
  
Happy trading,  
Ibo
