  * [#241](/thread/post/56772#post56772 "Post Permalink")

  * May 10, 2006 3:04pm  May 10, 2006 3:04pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

bigballer,  
I have mentionned this I think before that totally forget about fundamental when you are using enough big time frames. Just some news can make flurries on market. Fundamental for stocks are so important. But when using enough technical instruments you just need to know if there is a very important news on the way? If yes you just take care otherwise they will mislead you. It is joky that some sites drastically want to interpret moves with fundamentals. Really it is not possible that for such trading types you indicate proper and exact levels to enter, to exit and to pose oders or stops. They are totally interpretable, means that good for nothing in practice. In other words, this is like mass and energy, in astronomical speeds, mass and energy are the same things. You are expecting a sell-off regarding GDP, on the chart you find a reversal pattern like double top. These are the same. I can read your mind that you now have a question: So we can nicely use the fundamental at least as a confirmation or a part of our strategy. In fact, theoritically you are right. But what about if you know that these are some that know the figures or tamper with them for many reasons? So thiese are the cases that you will lose just because of regarding intensively to fundamental. Remember that I told PRICE IS THE BEST INDICATOR. Because no body can cheat on it.  
  
I hope this helps, it's my personal opinion and any other suggestion or opinion is respectable.  
  
Happy trading,  
Ibo

The USD CHF is a good example of a tempting trade long USD that I choose for the time being to stay out of or short with the trend the next turn.

  * [ Mike Jolley](mike*jolley)

  * | Joined Feb 2006  | Status: Trader | [89 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=6383)

I've been faked out several times already by apparent pin bars. The best one was GBPUSD on 5/1. It hit my stop almost 5 pips exactly below the pin bar and then shot up to my stoploss. That was annoying.  
  
Of course, now the reversal signs are getting pretty clear. I don't think there is any dollar weakness left that hasn't been taken care of by this long anti-dollar trend.  
  
However, I'd say the market is sideways now. Most pairs haven't hit their major trendlines yet. I think I'll just buy low and sell high for a while.  
  
What's weird is that it looks like every single pair has reversal signals, even the ones that have nothing to do with the dollar. I like that EURGBP is going up; That's a much-needed correction.

IBO,  
  
  
Thanks for the charts – they were very helpful to look at. In addition, I enjoyed reading part III.  
  
  
I will take a stab at your question regarding how one might get a confirmation sooner rather waiting for the price to break out of the channel.  
  
  
Although it would be best to wait until it did break the channel, one potential method is to study and understand price action and price bar analysis. One of the most important things the market can do during a trading day is to continue along the path of either hitting new highs or new lows for the day. This would also include assessing the speed and momentum of the price movement. This in conjunction with support and resistance may provide an early insight of a change in direction. Of course you also use proper trade entry techniques, tight stops and trailing stops if you think a reversal is taking place prior to the pricing breaking out of the channel.   
  
  
Mike

IBO,  
  
I posted a 4-H chart of the EUR/USD. You are going to yell at me again for being aggressive, but thought I would post my thought process and gain your feedback again.  
  
One can clearly see the purple arrows point to a downward trend – we had three price bars to the downside, but analyzing the price bars, I could see that the strength of that downturn was losing steam. Price hit the bottom channel and moved upward – then we got the blue buy arrow.   
  
Blue buy arrow, price losing momentum to the downside, failure to break the channel, and strong trend up. I bought the pair at at the blue upward arrow, and closed the position out at 1.2810 for a 97 pip gain.  
  
This seemed to be what you were eluding to in Part III - re-entry techniques?  
  
Thanks   
  
Mike

2) should we use value of the arrow as stoploss or some other more reliable values?  
3) what are the best pp or fibo levels should we use for taking profit?  
4) is it a good exit stratety if we simply reverse the trade when the arrow in the opposite direction occurs?

  * May 15, 2006 8:46pm  May 15, 2006 8:46pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

1)you should wait.  
2)arrow is just a confirmation, there is no value for it.  
3)you should trail the price then we have targets, 1st, 2nd, 3rd and so on.   
4)No, you should wait for closing the bar with a contrary arrow.  
  
Good luck  
Ibo

  * [#270](/thread/post/58556#post58556 "Post Permalink")

  * May 17, 2006 4:08am  May 17, 2006 4:08am 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Mike,  
  
The violance of the oil and gold prices had the influence on majors. It is an errant price at the time and nobody can tell the right direction, but a breakout/down is very likely in case of breaking the nearest support or resistance. This is a situation that you should think smaller time periods, in fact try to close your positions before reversing. Look at the H1 time frame. 55SMA is the resistance that is the final barrier for eur. But Making a new high is a harder work, if it can not then falls will occur and maybe we have some surge and tests. In this market the high and low of days and their breaking is so important. Most of the time they indicate the direction of the whole day. In other word when the low of the yesterday breaks then we should think short.  
  
Of course 55/8SMA are not the suitable MA for H1 chart. I will talk later on about the best MAs shortly in the thread and in advance for private members.  
  
Ibo  
  

> Quoting ForexMike
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Thanks IBO...  
>    
>  You mentioned that if the price closed above the white line...that is the point for which to look for an opportunity to get back in and buy if the trend is up - correct?  
>    
>  Mike

> Ignored

  * May 17, 2006 9:31am  May 17, 2006 9:31am 

  * [ ForexMike](forexmike)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [77 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4310)

IBO,  
  
Attached is a current snapshot of the EUR/USD at 8:15 p.m EST.   
  
I currently do not have any open positions. I am analyzing this pair to determine a re-entry point. Here is my thought process – let me know if you agree or if you would approach this differently.   
  
The most recent blue arrow indicates a buying opportunity; however, we do not just jump in. In the case of this pair, I would feel comfortable buying this pair since the trend is still up and have not really seen any strong indication of a major reversal.  
  
I have found that I am more comfortable buying in this case if the short term stochastic is below the 20 range. In this view, we are currently at 73.   
  
For added analysis: the dark orange lines are that of a detrended price oscillator (custom indicator for MT4), which visually shows when the price will become overbought or oversold. I think that this indicator may provide a more accurate view of the overbought/oversold levels.   
  
Also just analyzing the current price of the last two bars, the price looks weak, but then again it is just the opening of the Asian markets.  
  
So from my view, I would buy only, but looking at this chart right now, I do not see a good entry point.   
  
Feel free to add anything…  
  
Thanks!  
  
Mike

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

Hello all,  
Regarding biballer and Mike's discussion I have to tell you that:  
  
1- Such indicators that make bands to show overybought/sold levels are useful for the hours of market that is not in a strong momentum and just sideways. You can easily use BB(Bollinger Bands) to buy at lower band and sell at higher band aiming few pips when price sideways. I tried this when I was a newbie and it worked. You can see the Vegas fib lines, why it is almost a month that don't work? Because it is not for a strong trending market. Of course on the basis of the strategy with that you should wait until market reverse and shows enough reversal indications.   
  
2-Most of time market waits for a catalyst. Usually this is fundamental. In fact I am agree with bigballer, but keep in mind that its extent is day trading till a new trend in longer time frames forms. Mike you have a good common sens of the market. This is one of the best things that a trader could have.  
  
PS: I am sorry that I can not discuss most of the time in advance about the price action of the day. It is not included in my program for the thread.In fact it needs some prerequisits that is included in private mentoring. This is a long way that private members will be involved.  
  
Rgds,  
Ibo

as ibo is so generous in creating the thread to help all of us, i gave up a large portion of my sleep last night by creating this EA with following rules:  
  
1) buy/sell at the current bar if a EJ_4H signal appears at the previous bar  
2) exit if specified takeprofit/stoploss reached or reverse the order when opposite arrow appears  
  
hope other members can help me to test it. i attach the executable for now but if other members can provide some constructive feedbacks, i could consider to put the source code so that we could all work together to improve the EA.  
  
chinplant

good point, currently the EA trades immediately after the signal bar closes. what i could do is add an option so users can either trade at openning of new bar or follow your suggested strategy of placing stop orders upon breakout of high/low of previous bar.

Well - I believe we're now seeing the long awaited reversal for the dollar...  
  
EUR/USD has fallen 200 pips in the first 4 hour bar alone.   
  
Ibo - any advice on how to trade this? We know that any unnaturally long bar needs to be dealt with in a careful manner, since a correction of such frothy trading is to be expected.  
  
The 30M chart's dual stochs are both showing oversold, while the 4H chart's stochs are heading down from overbought. My personal tack would be to wait until the price has corrected up (and the 30M stochs are back at 'overbought') then go short...  
  
  
  
\- Ian

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

Hello   
  
After days now there is close below yellow line. I just add one thing to iboersma's comment. There are differences between supports and resistances regarding their importance. In fact they have types. Here price found a support at S1 weekly and is going to make a retrace. But any bounce does not means sell-off market. I have told this days ago. **KEY LEVEL is 1.2660.** I don't discuss why and how we should find the key levels, because it refers to the types of the sup/resis. Totally Ian has a good common sens of the market. SO, buyers look at close again above yellow line and sellers will be confirmed by any close below 1.2660. SO the zone between 1.2660 and 1.2690 is the errancy zone and each execution in this is not recommended. In fact you should watch out your positions when price is in this area to close in time if you see reversing signs.  
  
Chinplat, well done. I think it is better that you give some explanation on how the kids should use this and what are the parameters. If you don't like to publish it for public and just want to work with some programmers let me know then I will make an environment that you can complete it.  
  
Good trading,  
Ibo

  * Edited 8:44pm  May 18, 2006 8:35pm | Edited 8:44pm 

  * [ iboersma](iboersma)

> Quoting senbanda
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hello Ian  
>  I saved it to my computer and then attached it to C:/ProgramFiles/MetaTrader4/Experts/Indicators.  
>  I do not know any other way.

>  the above method worked.

> Ignored

Senbanda,  
  
Do this:  
  
1) Download the .mq4 file that Chinplant posted yesterday for the EJ_4H EA. You will be prompted to either Save it or Open it. Select Open. Your computer should recognize it as a MetaTrader file and open your MetaEditor automatically.  
  
2) You will now see the source code open in your MetaEditor application.  
  
3) At the top of MetaEditor, you will see a File menu option. Click that and select Save As. Navigate to the Experts directory in your MetaTrader directory (not Indicators). Save it there. Now go to the top menu bar of MetaEditor and click the Compile button. At the bottom of the screen you should see a message after doing this that says "no errors".   
  
4) Close and restart your MetaTrader application.   
  
5) Go to the Expert Advisors section of your navigator panel and you should see the EJ_4H EA there.   
  
Let me know if this doesn't work for you.  
  
\- Ian

Ian,  
Ichimolu is good for daily and higher charts. Its bands as form precedently sometimes is not bad to be checked.  
  
Never forget your analysis. PRICE is the best indicator. Always define channels and sup/resis. Then you have a field with signs, imagine that you have a city without traffic signs, what will happen? You will get confused.  
  
A simple trend line analysis is attached. Get the complete snap in the zipped format.  
  
Rgds,  
Ibo

Senbanda,  
  
My EA doesn't show any lines when I load it. You will know that it loaded correctly by looking at the top RIGHT portion of your chart. If you loaded it, but either do not have the "Expert Advisor" toggle button on the top menu bar selected, or do not have the "Allow Live Trading" option selected in the Properties of the EA itself, you will see a little face with a frown ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f641.png?v=15.1) . If you loaded it and have set it up to allow for live trading (via the Properties of the EA) and have the Expert Advisor button selected (on the top menu bar), the smiley face will have a big smile. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)   
  
Are you confusing the Expert Advisor with one of the indicators by chance?  
  
\- Ian

  * May 19, 2006 1:55pm  May 19, 2006 1:55pm 

  * [ jkjk](jkjk)

  * | Joined Jan 2006  | Status: Trader | [5 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=5658)

> Quoting migamb
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Can someone explain to me how the STOCH chart works? I read thorugh the part of the document that talks about it and have a general understanding but I would like a better explanation, else can someone point me in the right direction. Thanks.
> 
> Ignored

  
I don't have much experience with this, but if you look on your metatrader chart under the help category, then Analytics, then technical indicators; there's a list of the indicators that come with metatrader and their definitions.   
  
Here is what it says about the Stochastic Oscillator -   
  
**Stochastic Oscillator**  
  
The Stochastic Oscillator Technical Indicator compares where a security’s price closed relative to its price range over a given time period. The Stochastic Oscillator is displayed as two lines. The main line is called %K. The second line, called %D, is a [Moving Average](mk:@MSITStore:C:\\Program%20Files\\StrategyBuilderFX%204\\terminal.chm::/ug_ind_moving_average.htm) of %K. The %K line is usually displayed as a solid line and the %D line is usually displayed as a dotted line.  
  
There are several ways to interpret a Stochastic Oscillator. Three popular methods include:

  1. Buy when the Oscillator (either %K or %D) falls below a specific level (for example, 20) and then rises above that level. Sell when the Oscillator rises above a specific level (for example, 80) and then falls below that level;  

  2. Buy when the %K line rises above the %D line and sell when the %K line falls below the %D line;  

  3. Look for divergences. For instance: where prices are making a series of new highs and the Stochastic Oscillator is failing to surpass its previous highs.  

**Calculation**  
  
The Stochastic Oscillator has four variables:

  1. %K periods. This is the number of time periods used in the stochastic calculation;  

  2. %K Slowing Periods. This value controls the internal smoothing of %K. A value of 1 is considered a fast stochastic; a value of 3 is considered a slow stochastic;  

  3. %D periods. his is the number of time periods used when calculating a moving average of %K;  

  4. %D method. The method (i.e., Exponential, Simple, Smoothed, or Weighted) that is used to calculate %D.  

The formula for %K is: %K = (CLOSE-LOW(%K))/(HIGH(%K)-LOW(%K))*100   
  
Where:  
CLOSE — is today’s closing price;  
LOW(%K) — is the lowest low in %K periods;  
HIGH(%K) — is the highest high in %K periods.  
  
The %D moving average is calculated according to the formula: %D = SMA(%K, N)   
  
Where:  
N — is the smoothing period;  
SMA — is the [Simple Moving Average](mk:@MSITStore:C:\\Program%20Files\\StrategyBuilderFX%204\\terminal.chm::/ug_ind_moving_average.htm#simple_moving_average).

  * [ ForexMike](forexmike)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [77 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4310)

Here is a trade I took the other day:  
  
Bought on 5/18 @ 1.5494 and sold the morning of 5/18 1.5567 for a 73 pip gain. The red and green horizontal lines on the chart designate where I entered and sold. The green arrow shows the point at which I entered – second blue bar above the 8SMA (white line).   
  
This would be a buy signal per EJ’s method as the 8SMA (which is sloping up (white line) is below the 55SMA (yellow).  
  
Although the price crossed and closed above the 55SMA, I did not wish to stay in the trade for the price movement seemed to be loosing some steam, and the 55SMA is a resistance level. I could have put a trailing stop, just in case the price keep moving up, but just took the profit. As you can see the price came right back down to the 55SMA.  
  
Mike

> Quoting iboersma
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Senbanda,  
>    
>  Do this:  
>    
>  1) Download the .mq4 file that Chinplant posted yesterday for the EJ_4H EA. You will be prompted to either Save it or Open it. Select Open. Your computer should recognize it as a MetaTrader file and open your MetaEditor automatically.  
>    
>  2) You will now see the source code open in your MetaEditor application.  
>    
>  3) At the top of MetaEditor, you will see a File menu option. Click that and select Save As. Navigate to the Experts directory in your MetaTrader directory (not Indicators). Save it there. Now go to the top menu bar of MetaEditor and click the Compile button. At the bottom of the screen you should see a message after doing this that says "no errors".   
>    
>  4) Close and restart your MetaTrader application.   
>    
>  5) Go to the Expert Advisors section of your navigator panel and you should see the EJ_4H EA there.   
>    
>  Let me know if this doesn't work for you.  
>    
>  \- Ian

  * [ ktrade](ktrade)

  * | Joined Sep 2005  | Status: Trader | [159 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=3624)

Mike, it's not an indicator but an EA for autotrading. It's saved to your "experts" file - not your "experts- indicator" file. Save. restart, open navigator, find under experts and **_drag_** to your chart. You should see a happy face w/o smile. When the markets are open , you'll see a happy face in the top right corner of your screen telling you it's operational. Oh, make sure in your options settings you've allowed "live trading".  
  
k

  * [ migamb](migamb)

I just saw now that you sold, if you see the attached chart again, you can see that still price is above 8SMA, this is aggressive and any close below 8SMA is a confirmation of downside. If you look you can see that you will lose 20-30 pips if choose sell below white line rather than selling aggressively. BTW Part IV that will be published this weekend will enlighten this set-up.  
In case that you use other additional indications that give the weight to one side, then I recommend using limit orders because they get the top and dips very excellent and need few pips of stops. Moreover in case of reversing you can get out with few pips or even break-even, Buy I think you know how you should be kin to estimate the reversal zone.   
  
  
Good trading,  
Ibo

  * [#353](/thread/post/60378#post60378 "Post Permalink")

  * May 24, 2006 1:51am  May 24, 2006 1:51am 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Although we have a reversal from a decent trend but the potential supports are so close to eachother,in case of a sel-off market the 61.8% that is 55SMA here will be the first target and you should regard the support trend line that is for a major trend, so I recommend close watching to trail your stop ASAP to break-even and close the position if you see any reversal candle bouncing form a support. But if you think that this is a pair that its candles are overlapping ones, you are right, in the run of a trend you can see that the price will retrace to white line, this is the time that you can enter short. BUT when price reached yellow line or support it is a better case because it is indicating a major trend signal and you have more chance to be a winner.   
  
NEVER forget the relations among the diverse pairs, EUR is like GBP so GBPJPY will be so similar to EURJPY, meaning that you can see EURJPY condition and if you don't see any supporting for that and market for EURJPY is sell-off this means that you have a good chance to sell rather than buy.  
  
Best,  
Ibo

Attached Image

![](/attachment/image/5521?d=1148403088)

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

Hello everybody,  
  
Today we had a very slight moving market, this is because of the hesitation of sellers and buyers, most of traders believe that the eurusd will back soon to its uptrend. Anyway, 1.2880/90 is the strong resitance that medium term buyers are waiting for its break, if 1.2660 breaks we may have a very sell-off market.  
  
In case that price is near one of these levels (1.2660/90 as support and 1.2880/90 as resitance) eye closely to pose the stop orders and not lose the opportunity to catch the market sharp move. you can see the ranging market, before any breakout/down. We can play old game of buy at supports and sell at resistances. Support your trades by taking the other complementry like daily pivots and candle patterns.  
  
Good trading,  
Ibo

  * [#362](/thread/post/60872#post60872 "Post Permalink")

  * May 26, 2006 8:14pm  May 26, 2006 8:14pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Hello Traders,  
  
Just I wanted to add:  
  
For weekly pivots it is enough that you onetime a week (preferably the first day) update the weekly chart. The same goes for monthly. Update the monthly chart first day of month and then you can use the proper monthly pivots for its 30 days.  
  
**NOTE:** Market is in a sideways and one of the key levels should break to start a new trend or continue the previous trend. Just you should keep in mind that targets must be limited and never aim for much pips. Preferably close your positions at the end of that day. The nest week should be a catalyst then we can plan for very profitable trades.  
  
ATB,  
Ibo

  * [#367](/thread/post/60951#post60951 "Post Permalink")

  * May 27, 2006 1:37am  May 27, 2006 1:37am 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Ishay,  
In MT4 when you are watching a chart say eurusd weekly then weekly chart for eurusd is updated. In other words if you want to update all the time scales for eurusd you should click the buttons of M1,M5,M15,M30,H1,H4,D1,W1, MN.  
So, just to update wekly and monthly charts you should push the W1 and MN button.  
  
**Example: in the picture below the H4 chart will be updated.**

> Ishay,  
>  In MT4 when you are watching a chart say eurusd weekly then weekly chart for eurusd is updated. In other words if you want to update all the time scales for eurusd you should click the buttons of M1,M5,M15,M30,H1,H4,D1,W1, MN.  
>  So, just to update wekly and monthly charts you should push the W1 and MN button.  
>    
>  **Example: in the picture below the H4 chart will be updated.**

Could you please give us more information about risk reward ratio that you use for trading?

  * [#371](/thread/post/61152#post61152 "Post Permalink")

  * May 28, 2006 3:37am  May 28, 2006 3:37am 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Ishay,  
risk-reward ratio is the proportion of stop loss to take profit. e.g. you enter a position with 20 pips of stop loss and 40 pips of take profit. Then the risk-reward ratio for this wil be: 20/40=0.5. The less, the better.  
  
Then The ratio depends on the target that you have in mind for your trades. targeting is a very vast issue in trading. So we need talk about the risk management and targeting method before.   
  
Have a nice weekend,  
Ibo

Hi Mike  
  
The ema_slope indicator measures the slope of the EMA (exponential moving average) that one is using to trade and gives a positive or negative value on a degree/angle basis. Very similar to the CCI incicator with the + or - 100. Good visual (but this is an individual thing)  
  
Please note that this inidcator is not part of EJ_4HR method and is just an indicator that doubletop trades with. Hope this helps?  
  
Happy trading  
MM![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f44d.png?v=15.1)

The greatest achievements are those that benefit others....

**NEW MEMBERS should attentively read the first post to be awarned of what to do and what not to do after joining us. As a very old agreement we never start a new thread and by this, we never distract the attention and focus on the method. We will do all our activities in the framework of this thread.**  
  
**ATB,**

i like that you teach your stuff in steps for a newbie to easily follow but I would reconsider giving you any money just for that.  
  
private mentoring sounds nice but who are you to teach? Vegas spent whole pages just to tell his story.  
  
i read your all 4 documents and it did not make sense that much and I am not even a professional trader.  
  
i do apreciate that you put some pieces to gether and show how to build a system from scratch to newbie. its better to learn this way than from $2000 closed code systems that bring nothing.

well, it does not matter that much where the indicators and signals are from and Ibo explains how to use them. maybe I was a bit too harsh in my previous post.  
  
i am currently working to implement all 3 Vegas methods into a decent EA with proper MM. As Vegas said somewhere he trades the method that best suits given situation and that it does not prefer neither 1h, 4h nor daily over each other. so my EA should deside which method to use in changing markets and how much to risk. A Bot will never outperform a skilled trader but it could prove itself to be self sufficient and that is what I am looking for at the moment.  
  
i don't have the time to stare at charts for 24/5 and even if I did I still would not want to do it. As Eurousdtrader said, short time frames are a lot of needless stress.  
  
however, the major problem and in my mind it is not addressed here enough is how to spot the wrong signals and exit in a timely fashion. probably Money Management will be discussed in the Part V+ documents. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)  
  
I need an EA to provide a base of building my FX trader career. Maybe it is possible, maybe not.

  * Jun 7, 2006 11:32am  Jun 7, 2006 11:32am 

  * [ zzz](zzz)

  * | Joined Apr 2006  | Status: Trader | [159 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=8259)

This is kind of an answer to the angry letter of piccolo. It is not that I am pro or anti, just a thought.  
  
  
  
I am interested to pick Ibo’s brain as much as I can, for example. One of the reasons is that he is definitely a foreigner so he thinks differently and may have an alternative view on the market.  
  
  
  
See, you knew all systems that Ibo presumably borrowed, and I am sure they were more than enough to make you a very rich and happy person already, if used properly. Then you are not busy any more because the market takes care of you.  
  
  
  
I am also working with another guy, who is consistently making dozens or even hundreds percents of his account every month. What he has on his charts? MACD with the basic settings, basic stochastics, PPs and 2 EMAs, and that is it. 10 pips a day, as he likes to say, and these tools is all you need to become a multimillionaire very fast.  
  
  
  
People who really succeeded developed something else, behind the scene knowledge, if you wish. Their secret is irrational. When they, for whatever reason, decide to share their secrets, read it through many times trying to get in between the lines. That is where the real secret is. It is not about what toys you use. It is about what is going on inside of you when you use them and no technology will help you here.  
  
  
  
Of course, this is just my humble opinion.  
  
Cheers.

  * [#412](/thread/post/64026#post64026 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 7, 2006 6:13pm  Jun 7, 2006 6:13pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Hello,  
Thanks for the notes,  
  
I think I have talked about this fact that I'd like to say 50 pips a week rather than 10 pips a day. When you tighten the numbers of the profits that you need to make for a living, you will have a trouble, because you will think that you have to get 10 pips each day and this will force you enter trades that are not good ones, why you don't say 1 trade a week with a target of about 100 pips or two trades a week with 50 pips of target for each?  
  
There is a big truth that we need to learn basics of day trading, because always we can not trade on higher time scales (like the recent market in majors) in a ranging market we have to day trade, get less pips but make several trades. Plus, all day trading concepts is a good tool to time the best entry when you are trading hogher time frames like H4 and daily.  
  
Close price is the most important price. Candle charts is one of the best charting methods that traders use. After closing each candle we usually have to check the type of candle (open/close price, range, is it a candle pattern like spinnig top, hammer, doji and so on). If you trade on hourly you have to check the market off every one hour during the sessions. In fact you will have a killing job and many traders (that I have seen) could not tolerate more than a year. Moreover smaller time scales are less technical and most of the time disappoint traders especially newbies that are interested in getting good results of what they have learned about trading forex.  
  
I recommend that you learn intraday trading basics but never develop your main strategy on smaller time scales.  
  
I hope this helps,  
Excuse me for this long letter,  
Best,  
Ibo

> 
> Disliked
> 
> piccolo,  
>    
>  What you need first is a good theripist, who can properly analyse your brain functions. I don't think you are capable enough for trading.

Hi All (including piccolo),  
  
IBO is free to express himself and to share his knowledge the way he sees best. Mindless attack on the work of others is **not** to be encouraged. Ibo has spent a lot of time presenting his material and it is totally **irrelevant** where he got it from or whose system he is presenting. Even VEGAS [that Piccolo refers to] said in his documentations that people should take his idea(s) and run with it. No one system is perfect and people should be encouraged to think outside the box (as often as possible). Development comes from taking what someone has done and adjusting it to suit your style.  
  
I have constantly come across people (mainly like Piccolo) who attack the work(s) of others without offering positive solutions or ideas. They go from forum to forum with their eyes closed and attack anything that is similar to what they have read somewhere else. I find it strange that Piccolo also asks for later versions of EJ_4HR method documentations??? All this is not important, what matters is that we keep sharing and working together to become better at trading.   
  
Happy trading all and **please** lets get back to talking about the markets. Any ideas welcome. Lets stay **FOCUSED**  
  
MM![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f44d.png?v=15.1)

The greatest achievements are those that benefit others....

  * [ zzz](zzz)

  * | Joined Apr 2006  | Status: Trader | [159 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=8259)

i found envelopes around 55 SMA helping me to determine eisier what Ibo refers to as a good distance between the MAs. just zoom out every currency pair you trade and find the best fit for the last several moves. I always keep envelopes on my charts, they are like a roadmap. so, if a currency is sitting in the top zone, the buy is questioning, and the same goes for the downside. same idea as vegas's fibo lines, but to me much simpler and more obvious.

> Quoting piccolo
> 
> Disliked
> 
> yes, it exits the moment first opposite arrow flashes (doesn't matter if it stays there).
> 
> Ignored

Thanks Piccolo. I was thinking that after it kicks you out of the trade, it then re-enters the trade if the price goes back to the point where the opposite arrow disappears. Since the arrow from the previous bar's close is still there, it enters again? Then if the price triggers another indicator opposite it kicks you out again, losing the spread each time over and over.   
  
If that is the case, I guess the big question is do we want it to exit at the first opposite indication? If so, it should not re-enter when the opposite indicator disappears. Perhaps re-enter when the original signal reappears.   
  
Does this make sense? ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)  
  
Thanks everybody

#  [](/thread/5672-ej4h-method)EJ_4H method

  * [#441](/thread/post/64821#post64821 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 10, 2006 1:59am  Jun 10, 2006 1:59am 

  * [ powerbase](powerbase)

  * | Joined Mar 2006  | Status: Trader | [9 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=6858)

I totally agree that one should wait for a clearer signal. However, 1.27 will probably be a strong resistance for the pair but given that price may be at an exhaustion point it is probable that it will break. One strategy could be to do a scalp like entry near 1.2685 as it approaches the 1.2695 pivot and then tighten the stop to break even as soon as possible. Though, this would be quite an agressive entry, their should be enough momentum approaching the point to make this a good entry which could position for a break of the downward channel and pivot which are coincidentally aligned. The other strategy would be to put your order on the right side of the downward channel where most of the orders are likely to be.

We really can not say a 100% instruction for entering opposit side, just I can say here that if the slope of 55SMA is steep then it is better never go to the contrary side, because fighting a trend is a sheer folly when you don't have anu other solid indication.  
Such indications are rare and they bear high risks, but when the market has a cyclical behavior then you can enter opposit side.  
  
Ibo

  * [#444](/thread/post/64862#post64862 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 3:21am  Jun 10, 2006 3:14am | Edited 3:21am 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Dear Members,  
  
As you can see recently eur broke through a support cloud. This happened after a killing ranging market. Moreover yesterday's fall was sharp. You should keep in mind that after very sharp moves usually traders hesitate to initiate any new trade or at least they never go opposit direction,  
  
Sharp moves happen because of very solid reasons and rarely they come back soon.  
  
Today was Friday and as the last day of the weekly business round and after a calm market in European session (that is the most active session) tradres prefered to stay aside, because they knew that after NY session there won't be any active market to move the price in their direction.  
  
Breaking such a long term sideways may be is a start of a new down trend and initiating a rash long positin, at least for today, was not a professional doing.  
  
Have a nice weekend,  
Ibo

  * [#445](/thread/post/64893#post64893 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 10, 2006 3:52am  Jun 10, 2006 3:52am 

  * [ zzz](zzz)

  * | Joined Apr 2006  | Status: Trader | [159 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=8259)

powerbase, it is funny: i kept 2 pairs of envelopes at first, too, but then decided there were too many lines and removed the inside pair. also, according to the Ibo strategy number 2 we do enter when the price sits at the very top, for example, if the 55SMA is pointing up. then, by moving up, 55 SMA creates new space for the price to move, so i would say in a sharp moving market it does not really help.  
  
  
  
i am also experimenting with an envelope around 8SMA to trail stops. if you zoom the whole thing out, you can find the setting that would keep you in the most of the resent trades and retracements. Keep them there, until they stop working and then readjust. It works only in the trending market: when the price goes up, it normally sits on the upline of the 8SMA envelope - then you drug your stop loss along the bottom envelope line and opposite for the downside move.   
  
  
  
i think envelope is a very simple and useful tool that, apparently, does not look very cool, so people are pursuing funnier looking toys instead.  
  
  
  
If you decide to play with stop/loss and 8 SMA envelope, please, tell me what you think. Again, those are only experiments for now, so be careful.

  * Jun 12, 2006 2:04pm  Jun 12, 2006 2:04pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

**EJ_Pivot_DWM:**  
  
It is an indicator to draw daily, weekly and monthly pivot points. To setup each one act as below:  
  
Edit/Input/MyPeriod  
Double click on the 1440 and change the number into:  
10080 for weekly pivots  
43200 for monthly pivots  
  
1440 is defalt number that will show daily pivots.

  * [ powerbase](powerbase)

  * | Joined Mar 2006  | Status: Trader | [9 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=6858)

I am more of a scalp trader myself, but Ibo's method has been helping me to think more long term in my strategic trading. The best advice that I could give in making sense out of this method would be to use it in conjunction with channels, trendlines, support, and resistance levels. Also, pay close attention to how price reacts around the MA's. Usually, the best entries are at or near the MA's or at the channel borders.

you are funny bigballer. say, vegas is making tons of money with his system. can you repeat that? if yes, why you are here? people are making tons of money with simplest systems, but it is not mechanical. there is always a gut feeling that you have to develop in order to get what they do and unfortunately it takes time, lots of it. even if you run a trading robot, you have to know how to use it properly. most of knowledge in trading is irrational, nothing works like 1, 2, 3 and here is the result. you may find hundreds of discussions on different forums, or hundreds of trading ideas in books but no system will work for you right away. it might for some time, but then when the market situation changes, it will stop. i am sure you know all this, according to your previous posts. you don’t like it here? try somewhere else and see if you get much faster and much better consistent results. i am sure you tried vegas. did you make lots of money with his seemingly simple system, especially with a recent chop? so, tell me please does vegas system work or no? what would be a proof for you? vegas himself making money? i am sure he somehow does. can you repeat that?

as I see it and as has been said thousand times.. there are people who will make money with any system and there are people who won't with da best systems around.  
  
it's all subjective and a good trader will override system calls and sometimes won't follow them.  
  
i give you a system, i give you a track record but you won't know that I don't take 30% of the calls seriously.  
  
and it really doesn't matter if Ibo is making money and how much.  
  
all systems and methods should be reviewed by yourself and keep only those with which YOU can make money.

**Dear Friends,**  
  
  
  
**This is the last week that I post here and will stop posting from ****23 June 2006****but never stop helping and answering your questions. I always appreciate your interest and will do my best if I could.**  
  
  
  
This is not because that I want to make money with any program, I never have had such a purpose from the very first day.  
  
  
  
This is not because that some of members insulted me. They got their answers by other members.   
  
  
  
This is not because that some guys are going to change this thread into a court that I am the suspect of this court. I gave you something as a gift and never got anything. Nowhere in the world, are people addressed for gifts.  
  
  
  
This is not because that the moderators addressed my claim about the "views figure" of the thread as a deceit. As a rule of thumb a thread with more than 480 replies must have bigger number for views.   
  
  
  
I have ONE solid reason that today I reached. What is that is not our discussion. I just post this to thank all friends that showed interests and always helped me by encouraging and thanking. I also thank all that gave their not so friendly opinions about this thread or method or even me.   
  
  
  
**I am happy to say that as our old talks I never stop helping and interested members never hesitate if they had any question. Just email me at**[[b]ejeddi@gmail.com[/b]](mailto:ejeddi@gmail.com)**and I would be happy to be a bit of help for you.**  
  
  
  
**Happy trading,**  
****  
**Ibo**

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

[quote=eurusdtrader]

I will stop posting here from 23 June 2006 but never stop helping and answering questions. You have my email address at the bottom of all the EJ_4H Method parts .

  
  

**Ibo**

\- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -  
**This is a forex trading system on H4 chart with attached indicators and templates.**

  
  
**Instructions:**  
  
1- You should use MT4.  
  
2- You should Update Monthly, Weekly, Daily, H4, H1 charts when using.  
  
3- You should copy the indicators in .../Meta Trader/experts/indicators folder.  
  
4- You should copy the indicators in .../Meta Trader/templates folder.  
  
5- As this is an easy-to-use method you just use templates to do every thing with this method.(e.g. ususally setup ej_4h for monitoring and when you are predicting market by pivots you setup ej_4h_wp or/and ej_4h_mp and after your calculation back to ej_4h to see the chart with less difficulty.  
  
6- Templates with the extention of "wb" are ones with White Background to facilitate preparing a picture for printing or other use.  
  
**_Abbreviations:_**  
  
ej_4h ------------------------ Basic template (setup)  
ej_4h_wp -------------------- Basic setup+weekly pivots  
ej_4h_mp -------------------- Basic setup+monthly pivots  
ej_4h_dual stoch ------------- Basic setup+dual stochastic oscillator  
ej_4h dual stoch_Lindsay ----- Basic setup+overlaid dual stochastic oscillator  
  
**_Important Notes:_**  
  
  
**1- All Updates of indicators, templates and documents will be done in this post (the first #1), just a notification will be sent as a new reply (post).**  
  
  
**2-The texts/posts in blue color are the ones that members discuss daily/current price action, forecasts and commentaries; so for shortening the duration of following the thread if you are new to thread you can neglect them for awhile. ( We do this not to distract or diversify the efforts of members by starting a new thread, so please be aware that no new thread related to this method should be started)**  

\- - - - - - - - - - - - - -

**Private Mentoring ****is** **NOT** **available at the present time, for more info email to**[[b]ejeddi@gmail.com[/b]](mailto:ejeddi@gmail.com)

I have another question regarding entering during a trend. Part IV of the EJ_4H Method, shows clearly how one should go about in entering after a Retrace. My question is the position of the Stochs. Look at the attached Stochs. Earlier on they both showed an upward "long" position, and then later contradictory directions. Does this mean one can ignore them and enter a "short" position if the Sell Stop gets triggered?

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#503](/thread/post/189278#post189278 "Post Permalink")

  * Jan 17, 2007 7:45pm  Jan 17, 2007 7:45pm 

  * [ eurusdtrader](eurusdtrader)

  * | Joined Nov 2005  | Status: Trader | [122 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4307)

Please keep in mind that Price is the best indicator so you should give more importance and priority to line study. Plus, old indicators like RSI, STOCH and so on have been designed for stock market primarily years ago and they can not be leading indications in forex market which has a considerable turn over in comparison with stock exchange market.  
Choose trades that are in the direction of main trend. As you can see short time EMA has crossed longer term one and the main trend is DOWN. Magenta bars' color confirms this fact. Last candles have bounded from EMA and have broken short term upside channel. Even you can fit a 1-2-3 pattern and all these indications call for a short trade. If you employ some line study techniques like fibo ratios I think you can find more reasons.  
One of the best usages of old indicators is divergence. A divergence + breakout indicate a probable trustable indication to enter a trade in the direction of the breakout.  
Old indicators will work better in range-bound market conditions.  
  
I hope this will help,  
Rgds,  
Ibo

  

> [Quoting Linus](/thread/post/188421#post188421 "View Quoted Post")

I began using it on demo since early December and recently went live 5 weeks ago. I've been using EJ, with confirmation help from 4H MACD ("400 Pip/month"), and support/resistance to help me make decisions. So far it's provided me with nearly +1100 pips over the past 5 weeks, and averages +120pip/week since december.  
  
I've got nothing but praise for EJ. I would actually be sitting somewhere around +1600 pip if I was more disciplined. USD/CAD this week, GBP/JPY, and EUR/USD previously cost me around 500 Pips from trying to catch reversals instead of just making trades with the trend, oh well ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1) I'm learning still.  
  
Rob

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar25587_4.gif) drick008](drick008)

  * | Joined Nov 2006  | Status: Setup - Trigger - Follow Through | [162 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=25587)

Hi eurusdtrader,  
Thanks for the compliment but I owe it to your system.  
When I started looking into Forex, around Jan. 2006, I was looking for a perfect system that will give me a perfect signal. I was wrong. I beleive an indicator or signal is just telling me their is an opportunity. The entry, managing, and exiting a trade is a skill that I had to master. Your notes gave me a lot of entry strategies. I even printed them out and highlighted a lot of lines, so during simulation I wrote down where I can get in and see if I'm right or not. From this, I learned how to add positions during a trend and how to get back in if the trend continues.  
GBP/JPY is the most profitable pair for me. Next is the GBP/USD. I see other pairs works fine but the return is much more on GBP/JPY and GBP/USD...pips-wise.  
I want to thank you and those who contributed to this thread.  
  
Rick
